--
-- Структура таблицы `ks_drops_bank_items`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ks_drops_bank_items` (
  `item_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `qty` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `updated_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`item_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

--
-- Дамп данных таблицы `ks_drops_bank_items`
--

INSERT INTO `ks_drops_bank_items` (`item_id`, `qty`, `updated_at`) VALUES

(9, 4, '2026-01-02 18:00:18');

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Структура таблицы `ks_drops_cache`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ks_drops_cache` (
  `cache_key` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `payload_json` longtext NOT NULL,
  `fetched_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `expires_at` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`cache_key`),
  KEY `idx_expires` (`expires_at`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

--
-- Дамп данных таблицы `ks_drops_cache`
--

INSERT INTO `ks_drops_cache` (`cache_key`, `payload_json`, `fetched_at`, `expires_at`) VALUES
('online_metrics_v1', '{\"count\":18,\"user_ids\":[2,10,11,27,31,36,41,57,59,61,63,85,86,94,99,106,109,110],\"whitelist_count\":0,\"known_groups_count\":0,\"unknown_groups_count\":18,\"fetched_at_ms\":1767529359311}', '2026-01-04 12:22:39', '2026-01-04 12:24:39');

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Структура таблицы `ks_drops_log_chests`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ks_drops_log_chests` (
  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `chest_item_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `consumed_qty` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `reward_type` varchar(16) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `reward_item_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `reward_qty` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `result_code` varchar(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `message` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `ip` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `user_agent` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_user_time` (`user_id`,`created_at`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Структура таблицы `ks_drops_log_claims`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ks_drops_log_claims` (
  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `drop_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `result_code` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `message` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `ip` varchar(45) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `user_agent` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_user` (`user_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_drop` (`drop_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_result` (`result_code`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_created_at` (`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_user_created` (`user_id`,`created_at`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=349 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Структура таблицы `ks_drops_log_transfers`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ks_drops_log_transfers` (
  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `actor_user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `actor_group_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `from_type` enum('user','bank','mint') NOT NULL,
  `from_user_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `to_type` enum('user','bank','burn') NOT NULL,
  `to_user_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `item_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `qty` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `note` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `ip` varchar(45) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `user_agent` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_actor` (`actor_user_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_from` (`from_type`,`from_user_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_to` (`to_type`,`to_user_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_item` (`item_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_created_at` (`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_actor_created` (`actor_user_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_from_user_created` (`from_user_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_to_user_created` (`to_user_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_item_created` (`item_id`,`created_at`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=8 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

-- Дамп данных таблицы `ks_drops_log_transfers`

--
-- Структура таблицы `ks_resources_log`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ks_resources_log` (
  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `actor_user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `actor_group_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `resource_type` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `delta` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `note` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `ip` varchar(45) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `user_agent` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_user` (`user_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_actor` (`actor_user_id`,`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_type` (`resource_type`,`created_at`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Структура таблицы `ks_resources_stats`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ks_resources_stats` (
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `resource_type` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `amount` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`user_id`,`resource_type`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Структура таблицы `stats`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `stats` (
  `site_key` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `table_key` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `username` varchar(191) NOT NULL,
  `total` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `week_key` char(8) NOT NULL,
  `week_count` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `prev_week_key` char(8) DEFAULT NULL,
  `prev_week_count` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `month_key` char(7) NOT NULL,
  `month_count` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `prev_month_key` char(7) DEFAULT NULL,
  `prev_month_count` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `updated_at` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`site_key`,`table_key`,`user_id`),
  KEY `idx_week` (`site_key`,`table_key`,`week_key`,`week_count`,`updated_at`),
  KEY `idx_pweek` (`site_key`,`table_key`,`prev_week_key`,`prev_week_count`,`updated_at`),
  KEY `idx_month` (`site_key`,`table_key`,`month_key`,`month_count`,`updated_at`),
  KEY `idx_pmonth` (`site_key`,`table_key`,`prev_month_key`,`prev_month_count`,`updated_at`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;
